<tr><td width="742"><h3><a href="https://github.com/vdjhel3785/djy/blob/master/gb/22/6/3/n13751359.md#1" target="_blank">澳洲住房贷款额或已达顶峰 下月恐跌0.3%</a><br></h3><a href="https://github.com/vdjhel3785/djy/blob/master/gb/22/6/3/n13751359.md#1" target="_blank"><img width="150" src="https://i.epochtimes.com/assets/uploads/2019/03/20190321-Chi-Jin-big-four-Banks-882420252-150x120.jpg" align ="left"></a>随着澳洲住房市场面临诸多挑战，今年3月份住房贷款的意外增长很可能是市场周期的顶峰。
